    61	
    62	impl TyExt for Ty {
    63	    fn is_unit(&self) -> bool {
    64	        matches!(self.kind(Interner), TyKind::Tuple(0, _))
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    fn is_integral(&self) -> bool {
    68	        matches!(
    69	            self.kind(Interner),
    70	            TyKind::Scalar(Scalar::Int(_) | Scalar::Uint(_))
    71	                | TyKind::InferenceVar(_, TyVariableKind::Integer)
    72	        )
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    fn is_scalar(&self) -> bool {
    76	        matches!(self.kind(Interner), TyKind::Scalar(_))
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    fn is_floating_point(&self) -> bool {
    80	        matches!(
    81	            self.kind(Interner),
    82	            TyKind::Scalar(Scalar::Float(_)) | TyKind::InferenceVar(_, TyVariableKind::Float)
    83	        )
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    fn is_never(&self) -> bool {
    87	        matches!(self.kind(Interner), TyKind::Never)
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    fn is_str(&self) -> bool {
    91	        matches!(self.kind(Interner), TyKind::Str)
    92	    }
    93	
    94	    fn is_unknown(&self) -> bool {
    95	        matches!(self.kind(Interner), TyKind::Error)
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    fn contains_unknown(&self) -> bool {
    99	        self.data(Interner).flags.contains(TypeFlags::HAS_ERROR)
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    fn is_ty_var(&self) -> bool {
   103	        matches!(self.kind(Interner), TyKind::InferenceVar(_, _))
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    fn is_union(&self) -> bool {
   107	        matches!(self.adt_id(Interner), Some(AdtId(hir_def::AdtId::UnionId(_))))
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    fn as_adt(&self) -> Option<(hir_def::AdtId, &Substitution)> {
   111	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   112	            TyKind::Adt(AdtId(adt), parameters) => Some((*adt, parameters)),
   113	            _ => None,
   114	        }
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    fn as_builtin(&self) -> Option<BuiltinType> {
   118	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   119	            TyKind::Str => Some(BuiltinType::Str),
   120	            TyKind::Scalar(Scalar::Bool) => Some(BuiltinType::Bool),
   121	            TyKind::Scalar(Scalar::Char) => Some(BuiltinType::Char),
   122	            TyKind::Scalar(Scalar::Float(fty)) => Some(BuiltinType::Float(match fty {
   123	                FloatTy::F128 => BuiltinFloat::F128,
   124	                FloatTy::F64 => BuiltinFloat::F64,
   125	                FloatTy::F32 => BuiltinFloat::F32,
   126	                FloatTy::F16 => BuiltinFloat::F16,
   127	            })),
   128	            TyKind::Scalar(Scalar::Int(ity)) => Some(BuiltinType::Int(match ity {
   129	                IntTy::Isize => BuiltinInt::Isize,
   130	                IntTy::I8 => BuiltinInt::I8,
   131	                IntTy::I16 => BuiltinInt::I16,
   132	                IntTy::I32 => BuiltinInt::I32,
   133	                IntTy::I64 => BuiltinInt::I64,
   134	                IntTy::I128 => BuiltinInt::I128,
   135	            })),
   136	            TyKind::Scalar(Scalar::Uint(ity)) => Some(BuiltinType::Uint(match ity {
   137	                UintTy::Usize => BuiltinUint::Usize,
   138	                UintTy::U8 => BuiltinUint::U8,
   139	                UintTy::U16 => BuiltinUint::U16,
   140	                UintTy::U32 => BuiltinUint::U32,
   141	                UintTy::U64 => BuiltinUint::U64,
   142	                UintTy::U128 => BuiltinUint::U128,
   143	            })),
   144	            _ => None,
   145	        }
   146	    }
   147	
   148	    fn as_tuple(&self) -> Option<&Substitution> {
   149	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   150	            TyKind::Tuple(_, substs) => Some(substs),
   151	            _ => None,
   152	        }
   153	    }
   154	
   155	    fn as_closure(&self) -> Option<ClosureId> {
   156	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   157	            TyKind::Closure(id, _) => Some(*id),
   158	            _ => None,
   159	        }
   160	    }
   161	
   162	    fn as_fn_def(&self, db: &dyn HirDatabase) -> Option<FunctionId> {
   163	        match self.callable_def(db) {
   164	            Some(CallableDefId::FunctionId(func)) => Some(func),
   165	            Some(CallableDefId::StructId(_) | CallableDefId::EnumVariantId(_)) | None => None,
   166	        }
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    fn as_reference(&self) -> Option<(&Ty, Lifetime, Mutability)> {
   170	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   171	            TyKind::Ref(mutability, lifetime, ty) => Some((ty, lifetime.clone(), *mutability)),
   172	            _ => None,
   173	        }
   174	    }
   175	
   176	    fn as_raw_ptr(&self) -> Option<(&Ty, Mutability)> {
   177	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   178	            TyKind::Raw(mutability, ty) => Some((ty, *mutability)),
   179	            _ => None,
   180	        }
   181	    }
   182	
   183	    fn as_reference_or_ptr(&self) -> Option<(&Ty, Rawness, Mutability)> {
   184	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   185	            TyKind::Ref(mutability, _, ty) => Some((ty, Rawness::Ref, *mutability)),
   186	            TyKind::Raw(mutability, ty) => Some((ty, Rawness::RawPtr, *mutability)),
   187	            _ => None,
   188	        }
   189	    }
   190	
   191	    fn as_generic_def(&self, db: &dyn HirDatabase) -> Option<GenericDefId> {
   192	        match *self.kind(Interner) {
   193	            TyKind::Adt(AdtId(adt), ..) => Some(adt.into()),
   194	            TyKind::FnDef(callable, ..) => {
   195	                Some(GenericDefId::from_callable(db, ToChalk::from_chalk(db, callable)))
   196	            }
   197	            TyKind::AssociatedType(type_alias, ..) => Some(from_assoc_type_id(type_alias).into()),
   198	            TyKind::Foreign(type_alias, ..) => Some(from_foreign_def_id(type_alias).into()),
   199	            _ => None,
   200	        }
   201	    }
   202	
   203	    fn callable_def(&self, db: &dyn HirDatabase) -> Option<CallableDefId> {
   204	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   205	            &TyKind::FnDef(def, ..) => Some(ToChalk::from_chalk(db, def)),
   206	            _ => None,
   207	        }
   208	    }
   209	
   210	    fn callable_sig(&self, db: &dyn HirDatabase) -> Option<CallableSig> {
   211	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   212	            TyKind::Function(fn_ptr) => Some(CallableSig::from_fn_ptr(fn_ptr)),
   213	            TyKind::FnDef(def, parameters) => Some(CallableSig::from_def(db, *def, parameters)),
   214	            TyKind::Closure(.., substs) => ClosureSubst(substs).sig_ty().callable_sig(db),
   215	            _ => None,
   216	        }
   217	    }
   218	
   219	    fn dyn_trait(&self) -> Option<TraitId> {
   220	        let trait_ref = match self.kind(Interner) {
   221	            // The principal trait bound should be the first element of the bounds. This is an
   222	            // invariant ensured by `TyLoweringContext::lower_dyn_trait()`.
   223	            // FIXME: dyn types may not have principal trait and we don't want to return auto trait
   224	            // here.
   225	            TyKind::Dyn(dyn_ty) => dyn_ty.bounds.skip_binders().interned().first().and_then(|b| {
   226	                match b.skip_binders() {
   227	                    WhereClause::Implemented(trait_ref) => Some(trait_ref),
   228	                    _ => None,
   229	                }
   230	            }),
   231	            _ => None,
   232	        }?;
   233	        Some(from_chalk_trait_id(trait_ref.trait_id))
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    fn strip_references(&self) -> &Ty {
   237	        let mut t: &Ty = self;
   238	        while let TyKind::Ref(_mutability, _lifetime, ty) = t.kind(Interner) {
   239	            t = ty;
   240	        }
   241	        t
   242	    }
   243	
   244	    fn strip_reference(&self) -> &Ty {
   245	        self.as_reference().map_or(self, |(ty, _, _)| ty)
   246	    }
   247	
   248	    fn impl_trait_bounds(&self, db: &dyn HirDatabase) -> Option<Vec<QuantifiedWhereClause>> {
   249	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   250	            TyKind::OpaqueType(opaque_ty_id, subst) => {
   251	                match db.lookup_intern_impl_trait_id((*opaque_ty_id).into()) {
   252	                    ImplTraitId::AsyncBlockTypeImplTrait(def, _expr) => {
   253	                        let krate = def.module(db).krate();
   254	                        if let Some(future_trait) = LangItem::Future.resolve_trait(db, krate) {
   255	                            // This is only used by type walking.
   256	                            // Parameters will be walked outside, and projection predicate is not used.
   257	                            // So just provide the Future trait.
   258	                            let impl_bound = Binders::empty(
   259	                                Interner,
   260	                                WhereClause::Implemented(TraitRef {
   261	                                    trait_id: to_chalk_trait_id(future_trait),
   262	                                    substitution: Substitution::empty(Interner),
   263	                                }),
   264	                            );
   265	                            Some(vec![impl_bound])
   266	                        } else {
   267	                            None
   268	                        }
   269	                    }
   270	                    ImplTraitId::ReturnTypeImplTrait(func, idx) => {
   271	                        db.return_type_impl_traits(func).map(|it| {
   272	                            let data =
   273	                                (*it).as_ref().map(|rpit| rpit.impl_traits[idx].bounds.clone());
   274	                            data.substitute(Interner, &subst).into_value_and_skipped_binders().0
   275	                        })
   276	                    }
   277	                    ImplTraitId::TypeAliasImplTrait(alias, idx) => {
   278	                        db.type_alias_impl_traits(alias).map(|it| {
   279	                            let data =
   280	                                (*it).as_ref().map(|rpit| rpit.impl_traits[idx].bounds.clone());
   281	                            data.substitute(Interner, &subst).into_value_and_skipped_binders().0
   282	                        })
   283	                    }
   284	                }
   285	            }
   286	            TyKind::Alias(AliasTy::Opaque(opaque_ty)) => {
   287	                let predicates = match db.lookup_intern_impl_trait_id(opaque_ty.opaque_ty_id.into())
   288	                {
   289	                    ImplTraitId::ReturnTypeImplTrait(func, idx) => {
   290	                        db.return_type_impl_traits(func).map(|it| {
   291	                            let data =
   292	                                (*it).as_ref().map(|rpit| rpit.impl_traits[idx].bounds.clone());
   293	                            data.substitute(Interner, &opaque_ty.substitution)
   294	                        })
   295	                    }
   296	                    ImplTraitId::TypeAliasImplTrait(alias, idx) => {
   297	                        db.type_alias_impl_traits(alias).map(|it| {
   298	                            let data =
   299	                                (*it).as_ref().map(|rpit| rpit.impl_traits[idx].bounds.clone());
   300	                            data.substitute(Interner, &opaque_ty.substitution)
   301	                        })
   302	                    }
   303	                    // It always has an parameter for Future::Output type.
   304	                    ImplTraitId::AsyncBlockTypeImplTrait(..) => unreachable!(),
   305	                };
   306	
   307	                predicates.map(|it| it.into_value_and_skipped_binders().0)
   308	            }
   309	            TyKind::Placeholder(idx) => {
   310	                let id = from_placeholder_idx(db, *idx);
   311	                let generic_params = db.generic_params(id.parent);
   312	                let param_data = &generic_params[id.local_id];
   313	                match param_data {
   314	                    TypeOrConstParamData::TypeParamData(p) => match p.provenance {
   315	                        TypeParamProvenance::ArgumentImplTrait => {
   316	                            let substs = TyBuilder::placeholder_subst(db, id.parent);
   317	                            let predicates = db
   318	                                .generic_predicates(id.parent)
   319	                                .iter()
   320	                                .map(|pred| pred.clone().substitute(Interner, &substs))
   321	                                .filter(|wc| match wc.skip_binders() {
   322	                                    WhereClause::Implemented(tr) => {
   323	                                        &tr.self_type_parameter(Interner) == self
   324	                                    }
   325	                                    WhereClause::AliasEq(AliasEq {
   326	                                        alias: AliasTy::Projection(proj),
   327	                                        ty: _,
   328	                                    }) => &proj.self_type_parameter(db) == self,
   329	                                    WhereClause::TypeOutlives(TypeOutlives { ty, lifetime: _ }) => {
   330	                                        ty == self
   331	                                    }
   332	                                    _ => false,
   333	                                })
   334	                                .collect::<Vec<_>>();
   335	
   336	                            Some(predicates)
   337	                        }
   338	                        _ => None,
   339	                    },
   340	                    _ => None,
   341	                }
   342	            }
   343	            _ => None,
   344	        }
   345	    }
   346	
   347	    fn associated_type_parent_trait(&self, db: &dyn HirDatabase) -> Option<TraitId> {
   348	        match self.kind(Interner) {
   349	            TyKind::AssociatedType(id, ..) => match from_assoc_type_id(*id).lookup(db).container {
   350	                ItemContainerId::TraitId(trait_id) => Some(trait_id),
   351	                _ => None,
   352	            },
   353	            TyKind::Alias(AliasTy::Projection(projection_ty)) => {
   354	                match from_assoc_type_id(projection_ty.associated_ty_id).lookup(db).container {
   355	                    ItemContainerId::TraitId(trait_id) => Some(trait_id),
   356	                    _ => None,
   357	                }
   358	            }
   359	            _ => None,
   360	        }
   361	    }
   362	
   363	    fn is_copy(self, db: &dyn HirDatabase, owner: DefWithBodyId) -> bool {
   364	        let crate_id = owner.module(db).krate();
   365	        let Some(copy_trait) = LangItem::Copy.resolve_trait(db, crate_id) else {
   366	            return false;
   367	        };
   368	        let trait_ref = TyBuilder::trait_ref(db, copy_trait).push(self).build();
   369	        let env = db.trait_environment_for_body(owner);
   370	        let goal = Canonical {
   371	            value: InEnvironment::new(&env.env, trait_ref.cast(Interner)),
   372	            binders: CanonicalVarKinds::empty(Interner),
   373	        };
   374	        db.trait_solve(crate_id, None, goal).is_some()
   375	    }
   376	
   377	    fn equals_ctor(&self, other: &Ty) -> bool {
   378	        match (self.kind(Interner), other.kind(Interner)) {
   379	            (TyKind::Adt(adt, ..), TyKind::Adt(adt2, ..)) => adt == adt2,
   380	            (TyKind::Slice(_), TyKind::Slice(_)) | (TyKind::Array(_, _), TyKind::Array(_, _)) => {
   381	                true
   382	            }

+enum State {
+    Stop(()),
+}
+
+impl State {
+    fn get_or_init(&mut self) -> &mut () {
+        match self {
+            State::Stop(_) => {
+                let this = self;
+                let Self::Stop(f) = this else { unreachable!() };
+                *self = $0;
+            },
+        }
+    }
+}
+"#,
+        expect![[r#"
+            en State
+            ct Self
+            me get_or_init() fn(&mut self) -> &mut ()
+            lc f             ()
+            lc this          &mut State
+        "#]],
+    );
